Python Code python
import os import json # Now let's extract the actual content to find the common two-word model type print("=== EXTRACTING MODEL TYPES FROM RESEARCH FILES ===") # 1. Extract methodologies from PS Fader comprehensive analysis print("\n1. EXTRACTING PS FADER METHODOLOGIES:") with open('workspace/ps_fader_comprehensive_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: fader_data = json.load(f) fader_methodologies = set() # Extract from detailed_analysis print("\nFrom detailed analysis:") for item in fader_data['detailed_analysis']: if 'methodologies_mentioned' in item and item['methodologies_mentioned']: for method in item['methodologies_mentioned']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") # Extract from high_relevance_publications print("\nFrom high relevance publications:") for item in fader_data['high_relevance_publications']: if 'methodologies_mentioned' in item and item['methodologies_mentioned']: for method in item['methodologies_mentioned']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") # Extract from bibliographic_report print("\nFrom bibliographic report:") for item in fader_data['bibliographic_report']: if 'methodologies' in item and item['methodologies']: for method in item['methodologies']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") print(f"\nTotal unique PS Fader methodologies found: {len(fader_methodologies)}") print("PS Fader methodologies:") for method in sorted(fader_methodologies): print(f" - {method}") # 2. Extract from Kashyap final literature report print("\n\n2. EXTRACTING KASHYAP METHODOLOGIES:") with open('workspace/kashyap_final_literature_report.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: kashyap_content = f.read() # Search for methodology-related keywords in Kashyap's report kashyap_methodologies = set() lines = kashyap_content.split('\n') print("\nScanning Kashyap report for methodologies...") # Look for lines containing methodology keywords method_keywords = ['model', 'approach', 'method', 'analysis', 'framework', 'technique'] for line in lines: line_lower = line.strip().lower() if any(keyword in line_lower for keyword in method_keywords): # Extract potential methodology terms if 'markov' in line_lower or 'chain' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('markov chain') print(f" Found Markov reference: {line.strip()}") if 'clv' in line_lower or 'customer lifetime value' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('customer lifetime value') print(f" Found CLV reference: {line.strip()}") if 'retention' in line_lower and 'model' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('retention modeling') print(f" Found retention modeling: {line.strip()}") if 'survival' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('survival analysis') print(f" Found survival analysis: {line.strip()}") if 'cohort' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('cohort analysis') print(f" Found cohort analysis: {line.strip()}") if 'rfm' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('rfm analysis') print(f" Found RFM: {line.strip()}") print(f"\nKashyap methodologies found: {len(kashyap_methodologies)}") for method in sorted(kashyap_methodologies): print(f" - {method}") # 3. Extract from comparative analysis print("\n\n3. EXTRACTING FROM COMPARATIVE ANALYSIS:") with open('workspace/ps_fader_kashyap_comparative_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: comparative_data = json.load(f) print("\nMethodological comparison section:") if 'comparison_framework' in comparative_data: framework = comparative_data['comparison_framework'] if 'methodological_comparison' in framework: method_comp = framework['methodological_comparison'] print(json.dumps(method_comp, indent=2)) if 'key_findings' in framework: key_findings = framework['key_findings'] print("\nKey findings:") print(json.dumps(key_findings, indent=2))

import os import json # Now let's extract the actual content to find the common two-word model type print("=== EXTRACTING MODEL TYPES FROM RESEARCH FILES ===") # 1. Extract methodologies from PS Fader comprehensive analysis print("\n1. EXTRACTING PS FADER METHODOLOGIES:") with open('workspace/ps_fader_comprehensive_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: fader_data = json.load(f) fader_methodologies = set() # Extract from detailed_analysis print("\nFrom detailed analysis:") for item in fader_data['detailed_analysis']: if 'methodologies_mentioned' in item and item['methodologies_mentioned']: for method in item['methodologies_mentioned']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") # Extract from high_relevance_publications print("\nFrom high relevance publications:") for item in fader_data['high_relevance_publications']: if 'methodologies_mentioned' in item and item['methodologies_mentioned']: for method in item['methodologies_mentioned']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") # Extract from bibliographic_report print("\nFrom bibliographic report:") for item in fader_data['bibliographic_report']: if 'methodologies' in item and item['methodologies']: for method in item['methodologies']: fader_methodologies.add(method.strip().lower()) print(f" - {method}") print(f"\nTotal unique PS Fader methodologies found: {len(fader_methodologies)}") print("PS Fader methodologies:") for method in sorted(fader_methodologies): print(f" - {method}") # 2. Extract from Kashyap final literature report print("\n\n2. EXTRACTING KASHYAP METHODOLOGIES:") with open('workspace/kashyap_final_literature_report.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: kashyap_content = f.read() # Search for methodology-related keywords in Kashyap's report kashyap_methodologies = set() lines = kashyap_content.split('\n') print("\nScanning Kashyap report for methodologies...") # Look for lines containing methodology keywords method_keywords = ['model', 'approach', 'method', 'analysis', 'framework', 'technique'] for line in lines: line_lower = line.strip().lower() if any(keyword in line_lower for keyword in method_keywords): # Extract potential methodology terms if 'markov' in line_lower or 'chain' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('markov chain') print(f" Found Markov reference: {line.strip()}") if 'clv' in line_lower or 'customer lifetime value' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('customer lifetime value') print(f" Found CLV reference: {line.strip()}") if 'retention' in line_lower and 'model' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('retention modeling') print(f" Found retention modeling: {line.strip()}") if 'survival' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('survival analysis') print(f" Found survival analysis: {line.strip()}") if 'cohort' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('cohort analysis') print(f" Found cohort analysis: {line.strip()}") if 'rfm' in line_lower: kashyap_methodologies.add('rfm analysis') print(f" Found RFM: {line.strip()}") print(f"\nKashyap methodologies found: {len(kashyap_methodologies)}") for method in sorted(kashyap_methodologies): print(f" - {method}") # 3. Extract from comparative analysis print("\n\n3. EXTRACTING FROM COMPARATIVE ANALYSIS:") with open('workspace/ps_fader_kashyap_comparative_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: comparative_data = json.load(f) print("\nMethodological comparison section:") if 'comparison_framework' in comparative_data: framework = comparative_data['comparison_framework'] if 'methodological_comparison' in framework: method_comp = framework['methodological_comparison'] print(json.dumps(method_comp, indent=2)) if 'key_findings' in framework: key_findings = framework['key_findings'] print("\nKey findings:") print(json.dumps(key_findings, indent=2))

Python Code python
import os import json import re # Perform direct comparison analysis to identify common two-word model types print("=== DIRECT COMPARISON ANALYSIS FOR COMMON TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES ===") # Previously extracted methodologies fader_methodologies = {'beta-geometric', 'duration dependence', 'model', 'retention rate'} kashyap_methodologies = {'markov chain', 'retention modeling'} print("\nPreviously extracted methodologies:") print(f"PS Fader: {sorted(fader_methodologies)}") print(f"Kashyap: {sorted(kashyap_methodologies)}") # Check for direct overlaps print("\nDirect overlaps:") direct_overlaps = fader_methodologies.intersection(kashyap_methodologies) if direct_overlaps: for overlap in sorted(direct_overlaps): print(f" - {overlap}") else: print(" No direct overlaps found") # Now let's do a more thorough text analysis to find potential two-word model types print("\n=== COMPREHENSIVE TEXT ANALYSIS FOR TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES ===") # Read all file contents for deeper analysis with open('workspace/ps_fader_comprehensive_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: fader_data = json.load(f) with open('workspace/kashyap_final_literature_report.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: kashyap_content = f.read() with open('workspace/ps_fader_kashyap_comparative_analysis.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: comparative_data = json.load(f) # Extract all text from PS Fader data fader_text = "" for item in fader_data['detailed_analysis']: if 'snippet' in item: fader_text += " " + item['snippet'] if 'methodologies_mentioned' in item: for method in item['methodologies_mentioned']: fader_text += " " + method for item in fader_data.get('bibliographic_report', []): if 'abstract' in item: fader_text += " " + item['abstract'] # Combine all text sources all_fader_text = fader_text.lower() all_kashyap_text = kashyap_content.lower() print(f"\nPS Fader text length: {len(all_fader_text)} characters") print(f"Kashyap text length: {len(all_kashyap_text)} characters") # Define potential two-word model patterns to search for two_word_patterns = [ r'\b(markov chain)\b', r'\b(markov model)\b', r'\b(survival analysis)\b', r'\b(survival model)\b', r'\b(retention model)\b', r'\b(retention modeling)\b', r'\b(customer lifetime)\b', r'\b(lifetime value)\b', r'\b(cohort analysis)\b', r'\b(regression analysis)\b', r'\b(regression model)\b', r'\b(statistical model)\b', r'\b(predictive model)\b', r'\b(probabilistic model)\b', r'\b(beta geometric)\b', r'\b(beta-geometric)\b', r'\b(duration dependence)\b', r'\b(hazard model)\b', r'\b(churn model)\b', r'\b(churn analysis)\b', r'\b(logistic regression)\b', r'\b(linear regression)\b', r'\b(machine learning)\b', r'\b(neural network)\b', r'\b(random forest)\b', r'\b(decision tree)\b', r'\b(time series)\b', r'\b(panel data)\b', r'\b(longitudinal analysis)\b', r'\b(cross sectional)\b' ] print("\n=== SEARCHING FOR TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES ===") fader_matches = set() kashyap_matches = set() # Search in PS Fader text print("\nIn PS Fader research:") for pattern in two_word_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, all_fader_text) if matches: for match in matches: fader_matches.add(match) print(f" Found: {match}") # Search in Kashyap text print("\nIn Kashyap research:") for pattern in two_word_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, all_kashyap_text) if matches: for match in matches: kashyap_matches.add(match) print(f" Found: {match}") # Find common two-word model types print("\n=== IDENTIFYING COMMON TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES ===") common_models = fader_matches.intersection(kashyap_matches) if common_models: print(f"\nCOMMON TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES FOUND: {len(common_models)}") for model in sorted(common_models): print(f" *** {model.upper()} ***") # Show context for each common model print(f"\n Context in PS Fader research:") fader_context = re.search(rf'.{{50}}{re.escape(model)}.{{50}}', all_fader_text, re.IGNORECASE) if fader_context: print(f" ...{fader_context.group()}...") print(f"\n Context in Kashyap research:") kashyap_context = re.search(rf'.{{50}}{re.escape(model)}.{{50}}', all_kashyap_text, re.IGNORECASE) if kashyap_context: print(f" ...{kashyap_context.group()}...") print() else: print("\nNO COMMON TWO-WORD MODEL TYPES FOUND") print("\nPS Fader unique model types:") for model in sorted(fader_matches - kashyap_matches): print(f" - {model}") print("\nKashyap unique model types:") for model in sorted(kashyap_matches - fader_matches): print(f" - {model}") # Also check the comparative analysis for explicit mentions print("\n=== CHECKING COMPARATIVE ANALYSIS FOR EXPLICIT COMMON MODELS ===") comp_text = json.dumps(comparative_data).lower() print(f"Comparative analysis text length: {len(comp_text)} characters") for pattern in two_word_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, comp_text) if matches: for match in matches: print(f" Found in comparative analysis: {match}") # Save results to workspace results = { 'analysis_type': 'Common Two-Word Model Type Analysis', 'ps_fader_models': sorted(list(fader_matches)), 'kashyap_models': sorted(list(kashyap_matches)), 'common_models': sorted(list(common_models)), 'conclusion': 'Common models found' if common_models else 'No common models found' } with open('workspace/common_model_analysis.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(results, f, indent=2) print(f"\nResults saved to workspace/common_model_analysis.json") print(f"\nFINAL ANSWER: {len(common_models)} common two-word model type(s) identified")
